After understanding my arrival time at the hotel, while arranging my itinerary reasonably, I was able to check in successfully as soon as I arrived at the hotel, without wasting time waiting for the room. This alone made me overjoyed and got a full score for favorability. ‚òëÔ∏è

This should be my third time staying at the InterContinental Haikou. The first time was the Huacai Huayu Hotel before it was renovated, and the second time was after the renovation. The experience was particularly good that time. Whether it was the elegant decoration or the staggered arrangement of high-grade gray and noble black, I could check in and take pictures at every place without being too picky about the angle, and I could take pictures immediately. This is also the least thing to worry about as a professional hotel check-in user.

The one-night check-in experience does require a bit of high requirements from the hotel staff. Even though it is a little regrettable, every employee's attention and greetings to us during check-out are a very good impression and we are retained again.

üòâ Parts that need improvement:
1. The welcome fruit was reluctant. I redeemed the welcome fruit with points on Ctrip. Maybe it was also because I was picky. A plate of plain mangoes really made it difficult for me to have a good impression (and two of them were visibly bad üôÉ). It would be better not to send it, after all, it does not match the InterContinental luxury 5-star service experience. Of course, I can barely accept the reply of the duty manager, saying that mangoes are seasonal fruits, so this arrangement is made. For hotel check-ins, I feel a little regretful. I really don't come here to eat fruit, but to take pictures, which makes me reluctant to post the picture. It was said that I would be given fruit the next day, but I waited for a whole morning and it didn't arrive. Later, I thought there was no need to trouble others, so forget it.
2. I took a shower in the middle of the night and found that there was no hot water. That night, the manager told me that it was caused by a sudden damage to the boiler heating equipment. That night, I also waited for nearly an hour and was able to take a shower at 12 o'clock in the middle of the night. To be honest, it might not be so troublesome to take a shower earlier. Moreover, it is my personal habit to take a bath when staying in a hotel. At around 12 o'clock in the morning, the water temperature returned to normal as the manager said.
3. The variety of breakfast in the all-day restaurant is not satisfactory, and it is indeed not as good as the first time. Of course, the restaurant manager also saw me wandering around and asked about my needs. To be honest, the variety may be due to the off-season at this time, and there are not many products, which made me suddenly feel that there is nothing to eat. The second is that I want to drink coconut green (I saw that the restaurant provided it on Xiaohongshu before), and the manager said that it has never been provided. Well, maybe Xiaohongshu is a marketing method. Originally, I still wanted to take a coconut green with the hotel logo this time, which is really good for pictures and posting. This time, it is indeed a little regrettable that the "coconut green" is a little bit. üòÇ

In addition to the above minor flaws, the overall service of the hotel staff makes me respected. The service experience of the executive lounge is one of the best in the hotel brands I have stayed in. As soon as I came in, I was greeted and asked what I wanted to drink. At the same time, they also took care of the inconvenience of the customer's luggage, and took the initiative to ask the porter to help me carry my luggage when I checked out. I have to praise Cassie, the executive lounge's sister, for her attention to details: not polite, not restrained, too square and decent, and maintaining the comfort of the guests. I have to admire the professional training of the lounge manager and the high standards for employees. üëçüëç

Walking downstairs to wait for the car, there was a kind and friendly elder brother (I didn't pay attention to his name) who was also a front desk employee who took care of my stay. It is worthy of being the signature of InterContinental's old employees. He took the initiative to ask about my stay and experience, and instantly smoothed out all the small flaws and discomforts of my previous stay. I think this is also my refresh of the temperature of "making guests feel at home and treating guests like relatives".

Summary: It is really difficult to demand 100% service from a hotel. After all, every employee is an independent individual. It is precisely because of their unique style and characteristics, humility and courtesy that the luxury, grandeur and connotation of InterContinental Haikou have been achieved. At the same time, it also makes me believe that it is because of you that InterContinental Haikou will surpass itself step by step and become better and more outstanding. üëçüëç

The best part is that I was given an upgrade to a sea view suite with kitchen. The room has a large balcony with a 180-degree full sea view. The facilities in the room are spacious and maintain a high intercontinental standard. In addition, my room has a kitchen with equipment. It is fully equipped with a range hood, double-head induction cooker, a built-in large refrigerator with a height of one person, a washing machine with drying, and the four kinds of tea provided daily are of good quality. The hotel breakfast is also rich in variety. At night, across the sea, you can see the neon lights of Haikou city. Take a look at the rainbow night view and look at the quietly moored yachts in the harbor downstairs. I enjoy the tranquility and feel closely connected with the city. Thanks again to Miss Sally at the front desk for her considerate arrangements and giving me a great experience during this trip.
